  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_657d16ed-85d0-444b-a6de-fdaa03ae1727'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText5312712969337512934" style="display:none"><b>Night time is the right time...</b><br /><br />Gwendolyn Kidd has met the man of her dreams. He's hot, he's sexy, and what started as a no-names-exchanged night of passion has blossomed into a year and a half-long pleasure fest. Sure, it's a little strange that he only appears in her bed at night, but Gwen is so sure he's the one, she just can't turn him away... <br /><br />Hawk Delgado knows more about Gwen than she could ever imagine. She's gorgeous, headstrong, and skittish about relationships. But Hawk is facing his own demons, demons that keep him from connecting with anyone. Yet when Gwen is drawn into Denver's lethal underground scene, Hawk's protective nature comes out full force. The problem is, when Gwen gets a dose of Hawk's Alpha attitude in the daylight, she's not so sure he's the one anymore....</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/584497877?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=time-waste">time-waste</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer584497877" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6955963101833583032"><b>-1.000 Stars</b><br/><br/>When I decided to read this book I thought I was in for something, at the very least, interesting if not mind-blowing, since most of my friends seemed to love it. What I got was a messed up relationship, a shallow(and idiotic) heroine and a hero who... a hero... um, I really don't know what to say about the hero.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407445375ra/10722725.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Reasons why the heroine was an impecile who should have died long ago:</u>
</b><br/><br/>1) She was having sex with a guy whose name she didn't even know. Not once or twice, but every week </span>
  <span id="freeText6955963101833583032" style="display:none"><b>-1.000 Stars</b><br><br>When I decided to read this book I thought I was in for something, at the very least, interesting if not mind-blowing, since most of my friends seemed to love it. What I got was a messed up relationship, a shallow(and idiotic) heroine and a hero who... a hero... um, I really don't know what to say about the hero.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407445375ra/10722725.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Reasons why the heroine was an impecile who should have died long ago:</u>
</b><br><br>1) She was having sex with a guy whose name she didn't even know. Not once or twice, but every week for 1,5 year!<br><br>2) Said sex was unprotected even though she suspected the guy had a parade of other lovers.<br><br>3) Her sister is in a ton of trouble which will lead at best in jail, at worst in death. Someone broke into her house. Someone set her father's house on fire. Yet all our brilliant heroine thinks about is dresses, shoes, guys.<br><br>4) The aforementioned guy knew everything about her even though she knew nothing. He had installed cameras at her house(without asking permission or informing her), he had her followed and he is determined she belongs to him, despite her protests.<br><br>All that even though he thought of her as a slut who all but dropped her panties to get his attention the first night, and then had sex with him without knowing who he was for <b>1.5 FUCKING YEAR</b>!<br><br>Despite these facts she is seriously considering a relationship with him because he installed her a security system(without asking btw), got her a pair of "dreamy" shoes and carried her out of a fire(and I know it sounds all heroic and shit but she could have easily walked out on her own).<br><br>I guess let's forget his creapiness an his domineering ways since he got her shoes!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402420ra/782171.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>About the hero...I seriously can't tell you anything about him because at the 40% mark, the heroine doesn't know anything except that he is hot, he has 3 brothers and he used to be in the army(all of which she learned in the last two days, not the 1.5 year they'd been lovers).<br><br>I love a possessive, hot, Alpha male as much as the next girl but all this girl has seen of the hero so far is stalker-creepy, not sexy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370657ra/723498.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Btw did I mention that this TSTL girl with the fish IQ, this serial killer's victim waiting to happen, this godawful STD's best friend, has 4 hot guys pining for her? And as if she wasn't pathetic already, she also pants after them like some desperate 40 year old virgin. Seriously!<br><br>And the writing... Don't even get me started about the writing,<br><br>After I read about 40% of the book I got a little afraid that idiocy is contagious and decided to drop it as a precaution.<br><br>PS. Did I mention that this guy had been breaking into her house all this time? She hadn't given him keys or anything like that.</span>

<div id="review_349372952" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/349372952" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/349372952?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=super-cheese">super-cheese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer349372952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1200321050187399077">This will be yet another review where I will show off my fine skills of prioritizing. Forget the hero, the heroine, or the story. We have other stuff to take care of first.<br/><br/><b>Character description taken from the book itself :</b><br/><br/><i>I didn't expect to see tall, broad, inked-to-the-max, long blond-haired Dog standing at the other side of the counter.</i><br/><br/>HOLD THE PHONE. No one bothered to tell me that Dog the Bounty Hunter was making an appearance in this book.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380936i/738034.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Then...just when I thought it couldn't get any more </b></span>
  <span id="freeText1200321050187399077" style="display:none">This will be yet another review where I will show off my fine skills of prioritizing. Forget the hero, the heroine, or the story. We have other stuff to take care of first.<br><br><b>Character description taken from the book itself :</b><br><br><i>I didn't expect to see tall, broad, inked-to-the-max, long blond-haired Dog standing at the other side of the counter.</i><br><br>HOLD THE PHONE. No one bothered to tell me that Dog the Bounty Hunter was making an appearance in this book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380936i/738034.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Then...just when I thought it couldn't get any more surreal, I saw this :</b><br><br><i>her sister, Ginger Kidd</i><br><br>Wait a sec...is there really a character named <b>ginger kid</b>?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380936i/738035.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Disclaimer : I adore red haired children. Parents of red-haired children, please do not send hate mail because I posted a picture asking for help for ginger kids. I was only pointing out that this is a term not often used for flattery and probably not the best name for a book character.</i><br><br>Aw, hell. Let's just kick this review off with the characters.<br><br><b>Hawk</b> - a.k.a. - <i>The eighties called and they want their Camaro back.</i> He's a hot man. I'm not gonna lie. The hair, the skin, the dimples, the boots, the multi-national heritage. He's like a taller version of the guy who plays Ranger in the Stephanie Plum movie. <br><br>Who am I to complain, really? Other than a weird fondness for mid-life crisis muscle cars, he's my kinda man. I don't appreciate that he put cameras in Gwen's house to spy on her (Really?!? You couldn't have monitored her from outside of the house?) but hey. He gives great sex and he's pretty to look at. Sometimes that's about as good as it's going to get.<br><br><b>Gwen</b> - a.k.a. - <i>Shallow, ditsy, fluffy girl.</i> How the hell did this woman manage to get three hot guys willing to wage war over her? I could not stand this chick. After reading a book as long as this one was (and it was looooong), all I knew about her was that she drank cosmos, ate copious amounts of cookie dough, liked expensive shoes, and collected little black dresses. FFS, I would not want to hang out with this woman in real life. She had the depth of a potato chip. Although, I guess I can say that her big hair probably worked well with Hawk's camaro. At least they had a retro theme going on.<br><br>Since I've already figured out that nothing major changes about the men in these books other than how they look and what their jobs are, I'm hoping that the future will bring greater variety in the female lead department. I want to see big personalities, not Sex and the City wannabees.<br><br><b>The Story itself was...</b><br><br>Up and down. The first 15% was a lot of rambling about pop culture and side characters who weren't really in the story. Then things took off for a while and I was interested. Then we hit a downswing again when a couple of turf war issues repeated themselves. Then we hit an upswing, then a downswing, rinse and repeat. Gwen and Hawk were never really a believable couple to me until after they got back together for the last time and <b>then it got good.</b> The last couple of chapters and the epilogue were excellent. It's too bad that it took almost an entire book before I got excited about what was going on.<br><br>What interested me the most were the side characters. I'm looking forward to both Mitch and Tack's books. I have the feeling that I might like those books better, so fear not KA groupie girls. All is probably not lost.<br><br><b>The terminology was...</b><br><br>Eh. I think I'm used to it by now. I get that KA apparently loves nickname usage, which is something I loathe when it's used excessively in books. But I think I know that it's just part of the package and you have to deal with it if you're going to read and enjoy these books.<br><br>The squishy belly thing was just odd though. Gwen's belly got squishy a lot. I don't know if she was turned on or having indigestion.<br><br><i>Every male character sounded the same.</i> I've noticed this in other books of this author's as well. The sentence phrasing is very stilted. I get that it's conversational, so I'm not knocking that, but it's highly unlikely that every single guy you ever come in contact with is going to talk in the same exact style. Especially when you have a commando, a police guy (or whatever Mitch was, don't remember) and a biker all speaking the same way. Last I checked, there is no universal guy phrasing.<br><br>Example : "I was another type of man, the type they are, I wouldn't hesitate gettin' in there and muddling your head by making my play."<br><br><b>However, there's always a silver lining...</b><br><br>As stated earlier, the last part of the book was pretty flipping incredible. The epilogue = outstanding. <br><br>It's a first book to a series. Sure, there were some flaws, but I think there's room for growth. The book entertained me well enough to keep going, and often that's good enough. I have the feeling that my feelings about the series will grow fonder as I continue on with the rest of the stories.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1200321050187399077" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_284527573" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/284527573" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/284527573?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer284527573" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5375082145368520898"><b> HOLY ALPHA MALES!!!!!!! </b> Yowza!!!! *fans self*<br/><br/>I'm surprised this book didn't self-combust from the degree of <b> utterly squee/drool/swoon-worthy, bossy, possessive, unapologetic, sweet, tender, badass, HOT UBER ALPHA males </b> in it!! I mean WOW! This book is pure over-the-top deliciousness!<br/><br/>This book has it all: to-die-for hero, a sassy, smartass heroine, lots of action, hot hot sex, secret lairs, badass commandos, badass bikers, badass cops, drive-by's, cosmo parties, family time, romance, a few mi</span>
  <span id="freeText5375082145368520898" style="display:none"><b> HOLY ALPHA MALES!!!!!!! </b> Yowza!!!! *fans self*<br><br>I'm surprised this book didn't self-combust from the degree of <b> utterly squee/drool/swoon-worthy, bossy, possessive, unapologetic, sweet, tender, badass, HOT UBER ALPHA males </b> in it!! I mean WOW! This book is pure over-the-top deliciousness!<br><br>This book has it all: to-die-for hero, a sassy, smartass heroine, lots of action, hot hot sex, secret lairs, badass commandos, badass bikers, badass cops, drive-by's, cosmo parties, family time, romance, a few misty-eyed moments, laugh out loud humor, alpha males out the wazoo and just general over the top fun!<br><br>If you are at all a fan of the Black Dagger Brotherhood books, the guys in this series are very much like the human versions of them. Epic alpha badasses!<br><br>You are kind of thrown right into the story. Gwen met her "Mystery Man" at a bar a year and a half ago. She was just sitting there having a good time with her friends when in walks this big, tall, smoking hot guy that she can't take her eyes off. And after an entire evening what trying to get his attention but being ignored, he gets up to leave and...<br><br><i> "I felt a warm hand on the skin of my lower back.”<br>I twisted my neck, looked up and there he was.<br>I held my breath and he asked, “You comin’ or what?”<br>That was it. That was his pickup line. “You comin’ or what?”<br>I went." </i><br><br>*swooooooooooon* Yeah... :D<br><br>He begins to come to her at night every few days, but never shows his face and always leaves before morning... and Gwen, just can't bring herself to end this "relationship" such as it is with her Mystery Man. But trouble brews right from the beginning of the story, namely with her very messed up sister getting herself into some SERIOUS trouble with the wrong people and Gwen is thrown head-first into Badass World where she comes face to face with her Mystery Man, Cabe "Hawk" Delgado and the sparks fly for real, in daylight.<br><br>Hawk literally defines "alpha"!<br><br><i> “You're bossy, arrogant, intrusive, annoying... "<br>His minor grin amplified.<br>See! Totally unrepentant...<br>"Do I have anything going for me?"<br>"... you can be sweet, you're a cuddler, and you carried me out of a burning building..."<br>"I'm a cuddler?"<br>"You spoon."<br>His brows went up. "That's important enough to be on your list?"<br>"Uh... yeah."<br>[He's grinning] "Fuckin' ridiculous what women think is important.” </i><br><br>The writing style is very real. Its almost written exactly as someone would speak or think. It flows quite nicely and ends up reading almost as if you are hearing the main character think out loud.<br><br>"Babe" has always been my favorite term of endearment that a guy can call a girl. There is something just so possessive, and sweet and swoony about it. But Hawk takes it to a whole new level. That one word can mean so many different complete sentences. It takes a good author to make you understand exactly what he means without him saying it with just one word :)<br><br>And Hawk is not the only Alpha in this story by far. He's the badass commando leader. But we also get to <s> meet </s> drool over Mitch Lawson: badass cop (serious swoon material - can't wait till book 3 to read his story), and Tack: badass biker leader among many many others.<br><br><i> ""Are you here to freak me out in any other way?"<br>"Nope."<br>"This would include asking me for a date," I warned.<br>"Babe, don't date," he replied.<br>"You don't?"<br>"Do tequila shots followed by 5 hours of sex count as a date? he asked.<br>"Um... no," I answered.<br>"Then I don't date."<br>I smiled at him.<br>Then, stupidly, I asked. "You can have sex for 5 hours?"<br>He smiled at me.<br>Yikes.<br>Moving on." </i><br><br>There is a little bit of repetativeness in the dialogue, and the main couple have one stupid moment where I wanted to throttle them both, but the smooth writing, badass overload, laugh out loud moments, action, tender sweet moments, and uber alpha males kept me turning the pages and not wanting to put the book down! <br><br>And talk about a HEA! Such a sweet epilogue!!!!! <br><br>*goes off to join the Kristen Ashley Support Group*<br><br>How I see Hawk and Gwen:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370883i/723829._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, go to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com">http://aestasbookblog.com</a><br><br>Or join my FB group: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-...</a></span>

<div id="review_381178810" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/381178810" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381178810?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381178810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9008352169283291364"><b>5 Cabe “Hawk” Delgado Stars!!! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&current=HAWK_zpsab761f64.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745169.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <u>I LOVE HAWK!</u>
</b> Just going to put that out there before I review this book! How can you not??? What a yummy alpha male! Okay okay now to the book...<br/><br/>A year and a half. Thats how long Gwendolyn Kidd has been sleeping with MM, her Mystery Man. A year and a half ago she heard these words at the bar...<br/><b>
  <i> “You comin’ or what?” </i>
</b> <br/>She took MM home with her that night, and now he makes regular weekly visits. Sneaks in at night, then disappears. <br/>Gwen is having some iss</span>
  <span id="freeText9008352169283291364" style="display:none"><b>5 Cabe “Hawk” Delgado Stars!!! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=HAWK_zpsab761f64.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745169.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <u>I LOVE HAWK!</u>
</b> Just going to put that out there before I review this book! How can you not??? What a yummy alpha male! Okay okay now to the book...<br><br>A year and a half. Thats how long Gwendolyn Kidd has been sleeping with MM, her Mystery Man. A year and a half ago she heard these words at the bar...<br><b>
  <i> “You comin’ or what?” </i>
</b> <br>She took MM home with her that night, and now he makes regular weekly visits. Sneaks in at night, then disappears. <br>Gwen is having some issues with her sister, Ginger. Ginger is bad news.<br><i>”Why me? Why? Just innocently being born and seven years later, zap! God curses me with the sister from hell.”</i><br> Ginger is in trouble and Gwen is threatened. She doesn’t know who to turn to, so she goes to the local MC club where Gingers bf Dog is. She meets Tack there. She catches his attention. She also catches the eye of Mitch Lawson, the detective on her sisters case. This same day, she finally sees MM in the light of day.<br><br>Hawk shows up at Gwen’s house to help. He explains things to her and stakes his claim to Tack and Mitch. Gwen is his woman. She’s a little confused about all this, especially the fact that he knows everything that is going on in her life when they only sleep together. She doesn’t even know his name. <br><i>”How do you know so much about me?”<br> “Sweet Pea, I know who I fuck.”</i> <br>Hawk is a bad ass alpha man. He is sexy, protective, bossy and hot as hell. How he answers a lot of Gwen’s questions:<i>“Babe”</i> and when he leaves its because he’s <i>”Got shit to do, babe.” </i><br> Their ‘first date’-<br><i> “Tonight, you in a little black dress and high heels, I’ll be there at seven thirty.” “Are you asking me out on a date?”<br>“Sweet Pea, I’ve been fuckin’ you for a year and a half.” <br>“I know.”<br>“So no, I’m not askin’. I’m tellin’. You, dress, heels, I’ll be there at seven thirty.”<br>“So you’re not asking me out on a date, you’re telling me we’re going on a date?”<br> “That’s about it.” <br>“You can’t tell me we’re going out on a date.” <br>“Just did, babe.”</i><br><br>Love Hawk! Just love him! He wants to make Gwen his. I also really like Gwen. She is funny and spunky. I like her attitude. She is hesitant to be with Hawk. There is so much going on in her life right now, with her family and all the drama. Gwen is still keeping Hawk at arms length. They both have issues from past relationships, but are willing to try to make it work. <br><i> “Do you promise to handle me with care?”<br> “Promise” he whispered<br>“Swear?” I pushed.<br>“Swear, baby.” <br>“You had a hand up too, Hawk.” I told him.<br>“Dropped it a while ago, Gwen.”</i><br><br>There is a lot going on in this book... I won’t go on and on just READ IT!!! Loved Hawk and Gwen’s story! It was super hot(no woman in their right mind would have kicked Hawk out of bed), lots of action(break ins, drive by shootings, kidnappings, fires...yeah), romance(swoooon Hawk), and steam! I will just say, I can’t wait to read Tack’s book because I kind of love him too!!! :D <br><br>Some of my favorite quotes (there were <u>so many</u> good ones!):<br><br><b>
  <i> “Sweet Pea, the way you eat means you got tits and ass. This is good because I like tits and ass.”  <br><br>“A year and a half. Totally fuckin’ missed out.”<br><br>“Cookie dough,” I explained. “My booty is carefully crafted from copious intake of cookie dough.” <br>“Whatever you’re doin’, sweetheart, it’s workin’, so don’t stop.”  <br><br>“You got it wrong, in only a weekI was already tied to you. I wal already in deep. It was only a week, but it happened, you didn’t see it and you wen in for the kill.<br><br>”  “You’re in deep with me, aren’t you baby?” I whispered to confirm my question.<br>“Drowning.” He whispered back. </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9008352169283291364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Hawk is actually one of the less intense heroes I've read from her as far as possessiveness is concerned. He had enough to play it up but he was pretty cool about it.... Well compared to someone like Knight that is lol The plot did lose me briefly but it wrapped up nicely. Gwen did not win me over like the other heroines have. I'd rate this a 3.5.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer261578242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10222344541342288452"><b>3 to 3.5 stars</b> <br/><br/>The three star rating is completely due to Gwen's annoying and nitwitted character. Not even Hawk, the swoonalishous hero, could fully save this book for me. <br/><br/>I really tried to love this book but the heroine just rubbed me wrong. Really, really wrong! I understand why Hawk was enamored by her, he's the hero after all; but I'm still trying to figure out why Mitch and Tack were so smitten with her. I just don't get it! Of all Kristen Ashley heroines I've read, Gwen had the least subs</span>
  <span id="freeText10222344541342288452" style="display:none"><b>3 to 3.5 stars</b> <br /><br />The three star rating is completely due to Gwen's annoying and nitwitted character. Not even Hawk, the swoonalishous hero, could fully save this book for me. <br /><br />I really tried to love this book but the heroine just rubbed me wrong. Really, really wrong! I understand why Hawk was enamored by her, he's the hero after all; but I'm still trying to figure out why Mitch and Tack were so smitten with her. I just don't get it! Of all Kristen Ashley heroines I've read, Gwen had the least substance to her character. And don't get me started on her (figuratively speaking) bed hopping. Ugh! I did, however, like the last 20% of the book, and the epilogue was fantastic! </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/277975880" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/277975880?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mimi Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mimi Smith" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith">Mimi Smith</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

<span id="freeTextContainer1597321940260024149"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote><b>Dear Gwen</b><br/><br/><br/>No, I'm not a stalker. Why would you think that? I just wanted to talk to you about all that's happened in the last couple of weeks. Since you're not available (aka won't meet me), I'll just lay it all here.<br/><br/>First of all I'm really sorry about Ginger. She has always been trouble, but I never thought it would come to this. Gangs, cops, FBI. I'm also very sorry you got caught up in it. But, really you could always see there's something wrong with that one...<br/><br/><i>“Ginger. A pain in my a</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1597321940260024149" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote><b>Dear Gwen</b><br /><br /><br />No, I'm not a stalker. Why would you think that? I just wanted to talk to you about all that's happened in the last couple of weeks. Since you're not available (aka won't meet me), I'll just lay it all here.<br /><br />First of all I'm really sorry about Ginger. She has always been trouble, but I never thought it would come to this. Gangs, cops, FBI. I'm also very sorry you got caught up in it. But, really you could always see there's something wrong with that one...<br /><br /><i>“Ginger. A pain in my ass. A pain in my ass since the day she cut off all the hair on my Barbies. She was three. I was too old for Barbies but they were mine. She couldn’t leave them alone? What’s with cutting their hair?” I looked up at Dog and said, “I think that’s what psychos do. We should have known then. She’s three, wielding scissors and causing mayhem and heartbreak.” I kept blabbing as I dug in my purse, found my checkbook and then kept scrounging for a pen declaring, “She was always, always a bad seed.”</i><br /><br />Now, I know you girls have settled your problems, so I'll let off that one.<br /><br />About your Mystery Man. Sweety, a year and a half? Even leaving with him at the bar, after four words spoken is too much. He could've been a serial killer, a psycho! And then, letting him come for so long, just for sex, not knowing his name or anything? That's not all right, girl. Especially since he knew, like, everything. Oh, and don't even get me started on the lack of protection. You don't even know his name...STD, anyone? I know you had Sex Ed, girl. You need to take care of yourself.<br /><br /><i>I didn’t even give him a key. How he got in was as much a mystery as his name. But he did. He didn’t come every night, sometimes it was once a week, sometimes twice, sometimes he’d skip a week, once he’d been gone for three which freaked me out and then it freaked me out that it freaked me out.</i><br /><br />And, that wasn't a clue for you to do something?<br /><br />Well, I guess the Ginger incident was good for something. It brought you Hawk. And it could've gotten you Mitch or Tack, too. They're all such hunks. What on Earth did you do to get them interested? I can't get one guy, and you got three (4 counting Troy), just by talking to them for a minute! And they're willing to start a war for you or something! I'm sorry, I just found that hard to believe. Just tell me, did you slip them something? 'Cause, if you did I want it. And I think you flitted to them, when you and Hawk had problems, too often. You like a guy and have momentary problems, you sit down and talk to him, you don't jump to another guy's bike and hide. Geez!<br /><br />Still, I'm glad to see he conquered your defense system. You always ran from intimacy, even with him (hence the biker escapade), so I'm glad he saw that and dealt with it. I think you both made some mistakes (you ran when just a hint of a problem showed up, he was, well, Hawk), but I think your love is beautiful. And it was so fun going through all those things with you.<br /><br /><i>“Sweet Pea, what do you think I do for a living?”<br />“Well,” I started. “You fly on your supersonic jet to hot, humid, tropical, war torn nations, execute your duties as a soldier for hire which means doing things like blowing up bridges and beating infidels into submission.”<br />“Hard to do that and get home to take you to dinner,” he noted.<br />“Hawk, your jet is supersonic,” I reminded him.</i><br /><br />All in all, I think you're a great gal, funny as hell, and damn lucky to have Cabe.<br /><br />Now, because Hawk is a controlling SOB, and is probably afraid this letter is actually just a scam, and holds anthrax or something, he's going to read it. So, I just thought I'd talk to him, just a bit, ok?<br /><br /><b>Dear Hawk</b><br /><br />You are one of the hottest guys I've ever met. You can be sweet, you buy your girl shoes and you're good in bed. However, there are moments when your bossiness and controlling tendencies win out, and you cross the line into being too controlling and bossy. She is her own person and this isn't the 12th century. You can't just make decisions for her, without talking to her.<br /><br /><i>“I have to do what I have to do to deal with my woman, not a man in your yard will lift a finger to help you.”<br /><br />“Gwen, baby, clue in. I was makin’ you mine. When I make a woman mine, I do my homework.”</i><br /><br />And that gig at the start, you put cameras on her and had daily reports? Why not just talk to her, for Chrissake? That was just weird. And you're right, that year and a half-totally missed out.<br /><br />I'm very sorry about everything that happened to you and I'm glad you found Gwennie. Keep her happy, keep her safe, and try to control her cookie dough obsession...<br /><br /><b>Love, Mimi</b><br /><br />P.S-you might ask yourself how I know all this. That's ok, keep asking. </blockquote><br /><br />------------------------------------------<br /><br />And I know this totally breaks the concept but I had to put it here:<br /><br /><i>The newspapers had broken the stories of their adventures, and their love lives, some time ago. This was followed by a bunch of books, a series entitled Rock Chick, that were released sharing intimate detail of these hair-raising yet romantic adventures. Books, incidentally, I owned, read repeatedly and wished I’d edited.</i><br /><br />I love Kristen Ashley for this. Self promotion, with a dash of humor about the editing problems.<br /><br /> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/279263085" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 3 in the series</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/278771417" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 2 in the series</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/336327385" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 4 in the series</a></span>

  <span id="freeText3769469654038062696" style="display:none"><b>PACKING MY BAGS AND MOVING TO DENVER...YOU GET ME?</b><br><br>Once there, I'm finding an abandon warehouse tying myself up and waiting for Hawk Delgado to come rescue me. I went.</b><br><br>Gwen and Mystery Man have a sexual relationship for a year and a half. He breaks into her home at night and slips into her bed regulary. <br><br>The way this relationship plays out during this time is strange for this reader: #1: She never asks his name? and #2:She never speaks to him at all? <br><br>I would have been waiting at the front door for him or at the least left the windows and doors unlocked!<br><br>When danger finds Gwen the first person to show to protect her is Mystery Man. Then I breathed it out on a, “What?” “Clocked you before you clocked me, Gwen.”</b> <br><br>Gwen’s troubles land her the attention of other hot alphas: Tack from Ride and Detective Mitch Lawson who are interested in protecting her and winning her attention.<br><br>Conquering explosions, kidnappings and the Russian Mafia, Hawk fights through any obstacles for Gwen.     <a title="Splage" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4755656-splage"><img alt="Splage" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371778615p2/4755656.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/240510395?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Splage" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Splage" href="/user/show/4755656-splage">Splage</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=hero-heroine-widow-er">hero-heroine-widow-er</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4755656-splage?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer240510395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15511799254174444649"><b>Update 9/10/13</b><br/><i>Fabulous!! I have become a big audiobook person lately because real life is crazy and I desperately need my romance fixes!! This audiobook and narrator were spectacular, her voice totally nailed all the crazy personalities...it was SO MUCH FUN!! The story already is one of my favorites, then add the voice of the narrator and it makes the colorful characters and story even more enjoyable.</i><br/><br/>5+++ STARS -- A non-stop, wild ride! <b>Mystery Man</b> was the land of BADASSES and the testosterone w</span>
  <span id="freeText15511799254174444649" style="display:none"><b>Update 9/10/13</b><br /><i>Fabulous!! I have become a big audiobook person lately because real life is crazy and I desperately need my romance fixes!! This audiobook and narrator were spectacular, her voice totally nailed all the crazy personalities...it was SO MUCH FUN!! The story already is one of my favorites, then add the voice of the narrator and it makes the colorful characters and story even more enjoyable.</i><br /><br />5+++ STARS -- A non-stop, wild ride! <b>Mystery Man</b> was the land of BADASSES and the testosterone was overflowing everywhere, I would be surprised after reading this that I don't have hair on my chest. The story had an explosive romance and tons of action plus MAJOR BONUS! another gentle and perfect epilogue. I could see this one on the big screen - heck I could see many of KA books as movies. <br /><br />Hawk, the hero, was Gwen's mystery man and she had been his booty call for a year and a half. He had said like 3 words to her at a restaurant, I think they were"Are you coming?" After that he would just show up in her bed give her lots of "O's" coupled with wild romps and then be gone in the morning. Gwen struggled with her conscience and this pattern, but in the end gave in to it even though this submissive behavior was so far from Gwen's spunky personality. Then Gwen is threatened and dragged into a big mess because of her trashy sister's illegal actions. Gwen marches into a biker shop that houses a very dangerous biker gang to find out where her sister is. She catches the eye of the gang leader who is HOT! then is interrogated by a police detective who is HOT! and then her midnight mystery man shows up (who is HOT!) to scold her. Once Hawk opens his mouth to tell her she has just created a big mess she decides she doesn't like his high handedness and they are over...he shouldn't have opened his mouth. Hawk laughs at her, loves the attitude that she gives him and realizes how much he has missed out of over the pass year and a half with not getting to know her. Such parody, it was hysterical.<br /><br />Hawk was killer, beyond arrogant, I mean if there was a scale from 1 to 10 he would be like 100 and I mean arrogant not just confident. Enter Gwen, Hawk's perfect match, she didn't take his crap (except for the the first year and a half when he didn't open his mouth, at least for talking) At the beginning because Gwen had many other potential leading men, I wasn't even sure I wanted her with Hawk, but as the story progressed there was no questions. I actually think of all of KA alpha men that I have met so far Hawk would be their leader. Mystery Man also had so many other lovable characters from family to friends, a couple a different climaxes, some heart pounders, some heartbreakers--loved them all. I can't wait to read my next Kristen Ashley book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15511799254174444649" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer267789791" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15814433864173470244">5 stars – Romantic Suspense<br/><br/>All the single ladies, all the single ladies<br/>All the single ladies, all the single ladies<br/>All the single ladies...<br/><br/>Now pack your bags up!<br/><br/>Considering there’s not one but <i>four</i> yummy heroes introduced in this first book in the <i>Dream Man</i> series that’s set in Denver, Colorado (all of whom get their own book...YAY!), not to mention the smokin’ hot, badass alpha heroes from Ashley’s <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series, and it definitely wouldn’t be surprising if all the single ladies sudde</span>
  <span id="freeText15814433864173470244" style="display:none">5 stars – Romantic Suspense<br><br>All the single ladies, all the single ladies<br>All the single ladies, all the single ladies<br>All the single ladies...<br><br>Now pack your bags up!<br><br>Considering there’s not one but <i>four</i> yummy heroes introduced in this first book in the <i>Dream Man</i> series that’s set in Denver, Colorado (all of whom get their own book...YAY!), not to mention the smokin’ hot, badass alpha heroes from Ashley’s <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series, and it definitely wouldn’t be surprising if all the single ladies suddenly packed up and moved to Colorado.<br><br><i>
  <b>Mystery Man</b>
</i> is Cabe “Hawk” Delgado’s book. Initially, I was far more fascinated and smitten with Detective Mitch Lawson and biker badass Tack (two of the aforementioned yummy Dream Men who will have leading roles in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_" title="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a> respectively). But of course Hawk soon won me over and left me panting, daydreaming, and swooning like all of KA’s heroes.<br><br>Hawk is a growly, bossy, arrogant, brooding, domineering, and possessive uber alpha commando who could teach Tate from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227040.Sweet_Dreams__Colorado_Mountain___2_" title="Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a> a thing or two about being a badass, including the correct, standard rumbling response to anything and everything...<i>“Babe”</i>.<br><br>There were several times I wanted to smack both Hawk and Gwen, but they eventually got their sh*t together. Kristen Ashley is a master when it comes to dreamy, gratifying epilogues, and this time was certainly no exception...just heartwarming perfection. 5 stars!<br><br>Hawk<br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=ArmyHunk.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768612i/269684.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText17775487426699738591" style="display:none">I tried to stick it out because so many adore the series- but between the god awful dialog, "umm... Yeah". "ummmm". <div id="review_651399020" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/651399020" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/651399020?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Kristen Ashley Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer651399020" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6604717169896942642"><b> 5 Recognizing How Great This Was Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free<br/>QUICK BEFORE IT'S GONE, ONLY 99CENTS!!!</i><br/>When I first read this, it was during the binge of all KA. I think I had read <b>Motorcycle Man</b> and <b>At Peace</b> first... then did this series or <b>Rock Chicks</b>. I really can't remember right now. The reason I am bringing this up is to say...<br/> <br/><b>I Was Wrong....</b><br/><br/>Yup, I gave this a 4 star. It was during my thinking on the books I read while adding them to GR when I first came on. No reviews, just thinking back on</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6604717169896942642" style="display:none"><b> 5 Recognizing How Great This Was Stars<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free<br>QUICK BEFORE IT'S GONE, ONLY 99CENTS!!!</i><br>When I first read this, it was during the binge of all KA. I think I had read <b>Motorcycle Man</b> and <b>At Peace</b> first... then did this series or <b>Rock Chicks</b>. I really can't remember right now. The reason I am bringing this up is to say...<br> <br><b>I Was Wrong....</b><br><br>Yup, I gave this a 4 star. It was during my thinking on the books I read while adding them to GR when I first came on. No reviews, just thinking back on how I felt while reading them. The reason I gave this a 4 was the fact it had annoyed me Gwen had this guy come into her house for a year and a half and didn't ask his name or anything...just could not relate to it.<br><br>In Real Life, I still would never relate to that happening.... but now that I have read so much of KA, I understand the setup and reasons. <br><br>This book is PURE KA.</b> It is Vintage in all the wordy goodness she does. She will create an environment where kooky things will happen and you believe it. She has these Commando men... all hot, not a dud among them, and you accept it. <br><br>Gwen is smart- an editor (a nod to us readers), has her own girl posse, a back story which gives her vulnerabilities to overcome and sass. She is fully formed; has her quirks, has a complicated family history but a healthy relationship with her Stepmom and Father. So she is capable.<br><br>Throw her into this scenario of a hook up with Uber hot guy; brings him home and one drunken night turns into surprise stealth booty calls. <br><br>Add a messed up half-sister and visit from an equally messed up friend of said half-sister which causes Gwen to go to resident biker past boyfriend of half-sister to see what the hell is going on. <br><br>This, in turn, causes Hot Biker Tack to meet Gwen and put her on his "interest" radar... <br>Which causes Mystery Man Hot Sexy Booty Call to materialize in the Daylight for the first time to Gwen.<br><br>All of the above sets in motion a Perfect KA story with heart, sexy-times, sarcasm, terrific descriptions of houses, dresses, shoes, and men. It also provides deep revealing moments of both characters and insight into many circumstances that everyday people really could experience and relate to. <br><br>This is KA's Talent. She gives fantasy which has its core in reality. She does it extremely well. She does it so well that you are so deep into the book, you don't realize how committed you are until Real Life pulls you away...and you do not want to go and do whatever you are supposed to do.<br><br>So upon re-reading this book, I changed my rating from 4 to 5 stars. Also since I have been reading and now reviewing for over 2 years, had read more of her recent works...this re-read gave me a sense of what she has done in the past... and where she has been going and now writing. I would be remiss if I didn't say they are similar but different. They are diffidently her books, her voice...but the newer books have had even more personal focus then moving forward with action... maybe more introspective. Which isn't a bad thing... just different than these staples.<br><br>I loved reading this with all of my memories of characters that I knew more of because they had their own books...these characters' actions would ring true to me... cause me to think on them, too... adding to my enjoyment.<br><br>So, If like me, you have read these books, put them on your shelf, and continued your reading of other new books of KA.... then maybe it might be time to do a re-read...a refresher in why KA clicked with you...of opening that delightful discussion in your head or on a group here of who is your favorite Dream Man. <br><br>I am off to visit Tack...Oh, and by my re-reading this book, especially... I know I will get even more out of it... for I never understood the thing about "Peaches" and him... and now I do.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1483487036l/12299419._SX50_.jpg" alt="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/651399020">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12881141.Wild_Man__Dream_Man___2_" title="Wild Man (Dream Man, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1547157831l/12881141._SX50_.jpg" alt="Wild Man (Dream Man, #2) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Wild Man (Dream Man, #2)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/649577456q">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1547157881l/13412515._SY75_.jpg" alt="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Law Man (Dream Man #3)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/649577481">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_" title="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1547157943l/13448656._SX50_.jpg" alt="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Motorcycle Man (Dream Man #4)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/619911079">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43206597.Quiet_Man__Dream__0_5__Dream_Man__4_5_" title="Quiet Man (Dream #0.5;   <span id="freeText432631388223739379" style="display:none">Meet the guys... ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431199930i/14803582._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>

  <u>NAME:</u>
</b> Mitch Lawson.<br><b>

</b>Detective Mitch Lawson ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408662i/799626.jpg" width="400" height="466" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"Mitch".I whispered.<br>"What a perfect name ,soft and strong, things a cop need to be... Mitch."<br>He stared at me."Is it?", he asked.<br>"Perfect".<br>He stared at me some more.</b>
</i><br><br><b>
  <u>DESCRIPTION</u>
</b> With the perfect cop name that starts with 3 silent constables and ends with 'Lawson' as in 'son of the law.' Mitch is the hot-ass,soft spoken smoldering detective put on the case to bring down Gwendoline's little sister-from-hell 'Ginger' while sticking around to ensure he gets the elder to fall in love with him as well....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431199930i/14803582._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>ADMIRER #2 :</u>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>NAME:</u>
</b> Cabe "Hawk" Delgado. aka 'Mystery Man.'<br><b>
  <u>OCCUPATION:</u>
</b>secret-agent extraordinaire.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408662i/799627.jpg" width="500" height="334" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Don't call me baby when you're pissed, Sweet Pea."<br>"Don't call me Sweet Pea at all, baby.” </i>
</b><br><br><u>
  <b>DESCRIPTION:</b>
</u> Possessive,dominant and hot.Hawk is the definition of a beautiful nightmare.After maintaining a strict friends with benefit relationship for over a year with his girl 'Gwen',he's finally decided to come out in the broad daylight and claim her as his own...the outer whole world be damned.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431199930i/14803582._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>ADMIRER #3 :</u>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>NAME:</u>
</b> Tack<br><b>
  <u>OCCUPATION:</u>
</b>President of MC.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408662i/799628.jpg" width="480" height="312" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"Babe, don't date," he replied.<br>"You don't?"<br>"Do tequila shots followed by 5 hours of sex count as a date?", he asked.<br>"Um... no," I answered.<br>"Then I don't date."<br>I smiled at him.<br>Then, stupidly, I asked. "You can have sex for 5 hours?"<br>He smiled at me.Yikes....Moving on.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>DESCRIPTION</u>
</b>:This tall ,blue-eyed biker has got it all.Money,brains,power...and now he's decided he wants Gwen too.Tack's decided to take her as a challenge.And a challenge ? Well that's exactly what he lives and breathes for..its just that now its for Gwen too.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431199930i/14803582._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>THOUGHTS:</u>
</b><br><b>Mystery man</b> was surprisingly a fun read, that kept me laughing while swinging through the chapters from the beginning to its the end..Loved watching all 3 Alpha-Hot males fighting to win over our heroine,<i>Miss Gwendoline Kidd</i> aka 'Queen crash and burn' in all possible ways..whether they had to beg,borrow or steal...(or kidnap her in this case.)<br><br>I absolutely loved every secondary character, starting from the family members to her best friends,all who I felt came along and added their added personal touches to the final plot.<br><br><b>
  <u>Recommendation:</u>
</b>This book has only 5% of angst while the rest 95% consist of every other genre possible.Being a fun but long read.This ones absolutely recommended as an late evening read,for all HEA lovers.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/286496867?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer286496867" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7482764217352064510"><br/><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Gwendolyn Kidd and Cabe "Hawk" Delgado.<br/><br/>Ordinarily Kristen Ashley's books would not be the type of romances I'd read. Let alone enjoy. Gwen is an annoying heroine at times with really slutty behaviour. She sleeps with the hero for eighteen months and doesn't know his name. Then drools over not one but two other guys. The hero is a bit of a controlling alpha. The plot is OTT and pretty unbelievable. And I am seriously beginning to think that all Kristen Ashley's heroes went to the same sc</span>
  <span id="freeText7482764217352064510" style="display:none"><br /><b>2.5 stars</b><br /><br />Gwendolyn Kidd and Cabe "Hawk" Delgado.<br /><br />Ordinarily Kristen Ashley's books would not be the type of romances I'd read. Let alone enjoy. Gwen is an annoying heroine at times with really slutty behaviour. She sleeps with the hero for eighteen months and doesn't know his name. Then drools over not one but two other guys. The hero is a bit of a controlling alpha. The plot is OTT and pretty unbelievable. And I am seriously beginning to think that all Kristen Ashley's heroes went to the same school - "Babe". And all her heroines swam in the same gene pool - tall, long legs, big hair and all tits and ass.<br /><br />Entertaining as her books are, others may take issue with her writing style that often reads like an unedited draft with typos, rambling sentences and lack of punctuation. Be prepared for an enjoyable read, albeit at times frustrating and wordy.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 2.5<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7482764217352064510" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_243257028" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243257028" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243257028?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243257028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11920710691785588654"><b>UPDATE: Rating edited September 21, 2013. From 5 stars downgraded to 4 stars.</b><br/><br/>*********************************************************<br/><br/>Cabe (Hawk) Delgado said:<br/><b>"Don't have that chance so nothin' I can do about that. But I darkened your door, baby, and you</b><i> lit</i><b> up my life again, so I'm not lettin' that go."<br/><br/>5 stars.</b><br/><br/>Wow! Mystery Man is another great story and hilariously penned by Kristen Ashley! Kristen swept me right off my feet and directed me straight to reader's heaven. She does it all the time!</span>
  <span id="freeText11920710691785588654" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE: Rating edited September 21, 2013. From 5 stars downgraded to 4 stars.</b><br /><br />*********************************************************<br /><br />Cabe (Hawk) Delgado said:<br /><b>"Don't have that chance so nothin' I can do about that. But I darkened your door, baby, and you</b><i> lit</i><b> up my life again, so I'm not lettin' that go."<br /><br />5 stars.</b><br /><br />Wow! Mystery Man is another great story and hilariously penned by Kristen Ashley! Kristen swept me right off my feet and directed me straight to reader's heaven. She does it all the time! I can't help it but I just have to gush all the time.<br /><br />Cabe "Hawk" Delgado comes straight from Badass World. Hawk is another great alpha male and very bossy. On top of that, he is hot as all get out! And badass Hawk is locking horns with smartass Gwen! She is feisty, determined and can hold her own. Gwen, you kick ass! You will meet quite a few super hot guys in Mystery Man. Yeesh, the <i>hot-o-meter</i> was extremely busy and wheezing! <i>*wipes eyebrows*</i> I have to say that Hawk made a fine job in staking his claim. If there were any doubts yet then…<b>"Clue in, babe!"</b><br /><br /><i>"Friendly advice. Next time get your head outta your ass and stake your claim."<br />My body went solid but it still turned woodenly toward Hawk and I snapped loudly, "Hawk!"<br />Hawk looked down at me. "Man to man, babe, he's a man, he can take it and he's gotta know he fucked up."<br />For the first time in my life I was wishing murder wasn't illegal.</i><br /><br />When Gwen thinks about Cabe's job then she's got <i>that</i> on her mind (um, maybe she was joking, I'm not all that sure, though):<br /><br /><i>"You fly on your supersonic jet to hot, humid, tropical, war torn nations, execute your duties as a soldier for hire which means doing things like blowing up bridges and beating infidels into submission."</i><br /><br />The first half of the book is <b>absolutely hilarious</b> and the testosterone is all over the book. There were so many laughing-out-loud moments that I had to wipe my eyes. The dialogs were…<i>hilarious. Cool. Wonderful.</i> As always, Kristen does a fine job in developing and portraying all those wonderful characters. The plot got somewhat more serious throughout the second half of the book. Gwen had to unravel Cabe's secret. He is the Mystery Man after all. Hawk is protecting himself from pain and Gwen helped him to find his way back into the light. There's quite a bit of drama weaved into the plot - especially towards the end of the story.<br /><br />Ultimately, Gwen entered Badass World and Cabe entered Cosmo Girl World! YOWZA!<br /><br />Kristen, you were born under a lucky star! Keep the good stories coming! Honestly, I can't wait to read Mitch Lawson and Kane Allen's stories.<br />I totally enjoyed Mystery Man and if you want a good laugh then I highly recommend you to give this story a go! Enjoy!<br /><br /><i>On a personal note:</i><br />Gwen loves shoes; I am so <i>there,</i> babe! Mmmm…shoes to-die-for… *dreamy sigh* BTW, I love the way Kristen writes about clothes, shoes, furniture, and houses/flats. Seriously, Cabe's lair was the sh*t! Loved it!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11920710691785588654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1102336287" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1102336287" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1102336287?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

  <b>
    <i>“You’re livin’ in Badass World, baby,” he whispered in my ear. “Fair warning, until I fix what I cut in you, you’re there to stay.” </i>
  </b>

I just LOLed all the time.<br/><br/>If you follow my review you might know that I started my Kristen Ashley experience with the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/77851-unfinished-hero' rel='nofollow noopener'>Unfinished Hero</a> series and those books are essentially a two people cha</span>
  <span id="freeText1858044400322367756" style="display:none"><b>3.75 cookie dough solves every problem STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415826450i/11851612.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re livin’ in Badass World, baby,” he whispered in my ear. “Fair warning, until I fix what I cut in you, you’re there to stay.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>WHAT A HOT MESS!<br><br>There was so much going on, ups and downs and people getting kidnapped and shot at and so many characters. I just LOLed all the time.<br><br>If you follow my review you might know that I started my Kristen Ashley experience with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/77851-unfinished-hero" rel="nofollow noopener">Unfinished Hero</a> series and those books are essentially a two people character study.<br>That's why <i>Mystery Man</i> was such a complete surprise with all the side characters...and all the drama they brought to the table. Completely new experience and pretty interesting.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I felt a warm hand on the skin of my lower back.”<br>I twisted my neck, looked up and there he was.<br>I held my breath and he asked, “You comin’ or what?”<br>That was it. That was his pickup line. “You comin’ or what?”<br>I went.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It all starts out with Gwendolyn Kidd drinking too much, making googly eyes at the hot guy in the bar and eventually taking him home. Cue in super hot night of sex and the next morning mister mystery is gone. Oh well, it happens, right?<br><br>Not with this one...turns out he likes to come back for more. He comes back a lot! For a year and a half a few times a week the nameless man comes to Gwen at night...you can imagine the rest.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You're bossy, arrogant, intrusive, annoying... " <br>His minor grin amplified. <br>See! Totally unrepentant...<br>"Do I have anything going for me?"<br>"... you can be sweet, you're a cuddler, and you carried me out of a burning building..."<br>"I'm a cuddler?"<br>"You spoon."<br>His brows went up. "That's important enough to be on your list?"<br>"Uh... yeah."<br>[He's grinning] "Fuckin' ridiculous what women think is important.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Completely bonkers! Seriously. She doesn't even know how he gets into her house. HOT MESS!!!<br><br>Well, long story short...it takes for Gwen to get into some trouble with the local biker gang, thanks to her no good sister...and finally he shows up during the day and shares his name... which is Cabe “Hawk” Delgado btw, and pretty much turns her life upside down. And everything that happens next is just nuts.<br><br>I'm giving this book 3.75 stars, simply for being highly entertaining, messy and hilarious in all its fucked-up-ness. Of course the writing is excellent and I like the characters, but wow...what a trip.<br><br>All in all a nice read, with lots of alpha-male hotness, naughty shenanigans, drama and action and so many hot guys I couldn't keep count.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Are you here to freak me out in any other way?"<br>"Nope."<br>"This would include asking me for a date," I warned.<br>"Babe, don't date," he replied.<br>"You don't?"<br>"Do tequila shots followed by 5 hours of sex count as a date? he asked.<br>"Um... no," I answered.<br>"Then I don't date."<br>I smiled at him.<br>Then, stupidly, I asked. "You can have sex for 5 hours?"<br>He smiled at me.<br>Yikes.<br>Moving on.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>My biggest problem, or maybe you can call it the reason why I laughed so hard while reading is....*drum roll*... apparently the heroine has some sort of magnetic pull...I think they call it a golden vagina...literally every male character wanted in her panties. *head desk*<br><br>As I said <b>HOT MESS!</b><br><br><br><br>**Sorry for the short review. </a><br/><br/>This was my first KA book and BOY IT DID NOT DISAPPOINT!<br/>I kept seeing all over Good Reads all the rave reviews on so many of her books and more than a few of my friends told me to get on the KA band wagon and quick.<br/><br/>Well "Mystery Man" was definitely the PERFECT choice for my first endeavor into KA.<br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps5156443f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br><br>This was my first KA book and BOY IT DID NOT DISAPPOINT!<br>I kept seeing all over Good Reads all the rave reviews on so many of her books and more than a few of my friends told me to get on the KA band wagon and quick.<br><br>Well "Mystery Man" was definitely the PERFECT choice for my first endeavor into KA.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps5156443f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Gwendolyn Kidd has been having a hot affair with SEXY and ALL ALPHA MALE, Cabe "Hawk" Delgado for the past year and a half.<br>Sounds pretty amazing right?<br>Except, the only time they spend together is when Hawk shows up in her bed at night.<br>How he gets in, is a mystery to her.<br>Biggest Mystery is his NAME!!<br>She doesn't even know what it is!!!<br>OK...this sounds f'd up, but I was totally on board!!<br>Sign me right up for that deal!! <br>Amazing sex on a regular basis with a HOT ALPHA who can give me 4 orgasms a night AT LEAST??!!<br>Gwen met Hawk at a bar one night and took him home and to her bed, never thinking this thing would last over a year and that she'd still not know his name.<br><br><br>I loved this chick!!<br>She was a DOLL!!!<br>She knew this situation sounded totally f'd up and that it made her look like a whore and she owned up to it.<br>Her inner monologues were pretty funny.<br>This is one book heroine that I could get behind.<br>Never did she get on my nerves.<br>I found myself relating to her on so many things!<br>The girl loved her some cookie dough!! LOL<br><br>So things get pretty out of control for Gwen when her little sister gets herself in big trouble with some pretty shady characters. She has pissed off a lot of unsavory characters who seem to think that going after Gwen is the key to getting to the kid sister.<br><br>Now Hawk comes to Gwen's rescue!!<br>She finally finds out his name and learns this guy is ex military and runs his own type of security company.<br>AND the guy knows EVERYTHING about her!<br>He's been keeping close tabs on her this whole time!!!<br><br>Gwen has got to be the luckiest gal alive!!<br>She is surrounded by HOTNESS everywhere she turns!!<br>It seems that she has an effect on almost every man she meets.<br>We have Hawk, bad ass Commando.<br>Tack, HOT MC Biker!!<br>And Mitch Lawson, Gorgeous law man!!!<br><br>Let's throw in an undercover DEA hottie and some private investigators from the "Rock Chick" series, and all the gorgeous ex military men working for Hawk!!<br>I want a one way ticket to wherever this town is!!! Got that Babe??<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_mnz9w6B9nh1qdngmto1_500_zpsd27d5627.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><br>Gwen and Hawk grow closer during all the craziness as Hawk makes it his main mission to keep her safe, and he also makes it quite clear to all the other men who are in love with her, that she belongs to him alone.<br><br>This guy has suffered great loss and it explains why he was only the mystery man in Gwen's life for the past year and a half.<br>Gwen's had her heart broken and has been living inside her head for quite a while.<br>It explains why she was always "ok" with the relationship she had with Hawk.<br>But Hawk is seeing now that he "Missed Out" for the past year and a half, when he gets to know this feisty woman, who also can make him laugh like no other.<br><br>"Mystery Man" has tons of action, suspense, sexy scenes, a terrific heroine, and an ALPHA to top all ALPHAs!!<br><br>I can't say enough about this one!!<br>It was simply PERFECT!!!!<br>The Epilogue KICKED ASS!!! :)<br><br><br><b>I didn't even know his name.</b><br><i>

  <b>"A year and a half. Totally fuckin' missed out."</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>

Trust me babe, I know. I've been doin' near the same thing for awhile now, so long I forgot what it feels like to be alive. You got in my face that day you got back from Ride and reminded me what it feels like to be alive. Feels good, Sweet Pea, so I'm not goin' back now."</b>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1417378891" class="readable"
