<span id="freeTextContainer16807379163866936227"><b>Sale Alert: Kindle Deal May 4 – May 10 <a href='https://www.amazon.com/Mystery-Man-Dream-Book-ebook/dp/B00AHFJABS/ref=sr_1_83?dchild=1&qid=1588651592&s=digital-text&sr=1-83' rel='nofollow noopener'>$2.99</a></b><br/><br/>I always feel like I have to give this disclaimer with KA books but maybe even more-so with this one…<b> not everyone is going to be okay with this book or the heroine or the hero</b>. There are very specific reasons why that is the case but mostly it is because it isn’t your usual boy meets girl story. It’s more of a boy sees girl, boy thinks girl is hot, boy takes girl to bed and then sneaks into her house to pretty much booty call her for a year and a half</span>
  <span id="freeText16807379163866936227" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert: Kindle Deal May 4 – May 10 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Mystery-Man-Dream-Book-ebook/dp/B00AHFJABS/ref=sr_1_83?dchild=1&amp;qid=1588651592&amp;s=digital-text&amp;sr=1-83" rel="nofollow noopener">$2.99</a></b><br /><br />I always feel like I have to give this disclaimer with KA books but maybe even more-so with this one…<b> not everyone is going to be okay with this book or the heroine or the hero</b>. There are very specific reasons why that is the case but mostly it is because it isn’t your usual boy meets girl story. It’s more of a boy sees girl, boy thinks girl is hot, boy takes girl to bed and then sneaks into her house to pretty much booty call her for a year and a half without her even knowing his name.<br /><br />In most KA book I suspend disbelief because I always seem to like the emotional journey she takes me on. So while I can’t imagine being Gwen and seeing the hot stranger in a restaurant and taking him home without much conversation including the general niceties such as ‘what’s your name’ I totally love the dangerous idea of it. <b>Okay so real life totally not going to happen….but this is KA land</b> and in that world Alpha men have little to no boundaries and they sneak into your house a few days later for some of the best sex of your life and then continue to do that intermittently for over a year.<br /><br />Too bad her stupid selfish sister has to screw it all up and turn Gwen’s life upside down. After getting into a little trouble it seems that Gwen has been pulled into her sisters problems which also introduces her to many hot men from so different areas in life including H O T cop Mitch Lawson (totally going to read his book). I little flirting with him brings out night lovers slightly jealous side so that he wants to make a claim and make sure that Gwen knows she’s totally his.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Mitch,” I whispered. “Strong, the last three consonants, that is, but not in a harsh way, in a soft way. And when you’re with someone you care about and you’re close and they say something you can’t hear, you don’t say, ‘What?’ you say, ‘Mm?’ real soft. Put that and the last together, soft and strong, things a cop needs to be… Mitch.” <br />He stared at me. <br />I kept babbling. “And Lawson, goes without saying, Law… son. Son of the law.” I pulled in a breath through my nose and then whispered, “Perfect.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I LOVE IT!!! But it seems Hawk (previously unnamed nighttime visitor) is not happy about all the sudden Alpha males interested in his girl on the down low.<br /><br />Okay so there are a few things…..<br /><br />One….I was totally loving the story and the new relationship status that Gwen is having with Hawk even though she is really fighting that every step of the way and then KA dropped the emotional bomb on me and I WAS NOT READY…..and I hated Hawk. Yep you heard me…I hated him because he hurt her feelings so much with some of his other ‘activities’ while they were having night time visits, and by visits I just mean sex together. And Gwen killed me with her reaction when we all found out what the bomb was.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I want him,” I whispered my secret.<br /> “Then talk to him,” Cam whispered back.<br /> “I wanted him to be special,” I kept whispering. “<br />Girl,” she kept whispering too and got closer, wrapping her fingers around my arm, “talk to him….. <br /><b>“I’ll always be filler,”</b></i>
</blockquote><br />And Gwenny was totally hurt and I was hurt with her and Hawk was the biggest asshole around. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[okay he’d slept with other women in the course of their 1.5 year booty call and I was super mad at him for awhile. But…then I realized that she never initiated a single conversation in all the time they were sleeping together and hard to work out the acceptables of your relationship when you’ve never really talked to the man. Gwen could have changed her situation at any time. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I’m not saying I was happy about it but I’ll give it a pass this time based on the parameters of the situation.<br /><br />Two…..there are some H O T alpha men in this and all of them seem to meet Gwen and get an instant hard on for her. Like she must be putting off some serious pheromones for the amount of tuff guy interest in her. Still I’m going to allow it based on this being a KA book and that I enjoyed it. But seriously it’s like she smelled like a steak and they all wanted a big bite.<br /><br />Three….There are some great side characters. I loved all her friends and Elvira the secretary for Hawk’s place of work was the absolute best. She got away with saying some crazy fun stuff and just inserted herself into Gwen’s life like she’d been there all along. I totally loved it.<br /><blockquote>
  <i> “Who’re you?” Elvira demanded to know, eyeing up Cam and Cam looked at her.<br /> “Gwen’s best friend,” Cam answered. <br />Tracy had made it to the bar and she leaned both forearms into it, saying to Elvira, “We share that title.” <br />Elvira looked over her shoulder at me where I was positioning myself at the back counter. “If that’s true, girl, you better make up your mind ’cause you can’t have two maids of honor.</i>
</blockquote><br />Four….this is a bit alpha over the top even for one of KAs books so just be prepared and roll with it. Hawk is all alpha all the time and like many KA heroes he might be a bit broken so we all know that he will do something stupid because he doesn’t know how to deal with the situation. But I has some great intense emotional reactions in this to his backstory and how Gwen came to terms with both her past and his.<br /><br />Overall I enjoyed the story and while this by no means has any place in the real world the story for the most part worked for me and now I need to get to know all the Mystery Men.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16807379163866936227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText18296931076725401678" style="display:none"><b>Fourth read: February 8-16, 2017</b><br><br><i>Let me first state that the audio version is a 3 star rating and the printed version is still a 5 star rating.</i><br><br>This re-read started out as an audio review, but around the 49% mark I had to go find my place on my Kindle and read the rest of the book from there.<br><br>There are two reasons why I did this:<br>1) I could read this book faster than the narrator was speaking.<br>2) I didn't care for the narration. <br>Don't get me wrong, she did a great job of narrating the story, but in my mind how she was reading the characters was not how I heard them in my head.<br><br>This is one of my favorite books by Kristen Ashley, and I didn't want another interpretation of the story other than the one my imagination and mind created while reading the story.<br><br>Still a favorite, but I think I'll stick to the printed version. <br><br><br><i> First read: March 1, 2012</i><br><br>I really don't think Ms. Ashley can write a 'bad' book!<br>This was fricken Amazing!<br>Love Hawk &amp; Gwen, and her messed up sister, and the biker dudes, the 'Hot' cops, and all the Commando type guys<br>..... and where in the world do you find guys that talk all Neanderthal and answer 'Babe' like that's the obvious answer, but it still comes across as Alpha and Sexy as hell? <br><br><i> Second read: March 5, 2013</i><br><br>The last couple of days I have been re-introduced to Kristen Ashley's mysterious and fantastic world of Commando's, Motorcycle Bad-Asses, sexy Cop's, and Private Investigator's... and I FRIGGEN LOVED IT...AGAIN!!!<br><br>It has been exactly a year since I first met Cabe "Hawk" Delgato &amp; Gwen Kidd. In that year I haven't thought of them, but when I started to re-read their story it didn't take long for me to get caught up in them. <br>I LOVE their characters! I love that everything they'd been thru in their pasts &amp; the brokenness &amp; the walls they've put up because if it.... they were finally able to 'put their hands down' and begin to heal one another with their strength, courage, and love. <br><br>Once Hawk opened his heart to Gwen... that was it!<br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pictures%203/protectwhatsyours.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380367892i/720392.jpg" alt=" photo protectwhatsyours.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Their story and their ending is <br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pictures%203/beautiful.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380367892i/720393.jpg" alt=" photo beautiful.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>.. and the Epilogue had me in tears again. Cabe's sweetness towards Gwen and that bloody intimate kiss behind the ear<br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pictures%203/kissingneck.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380367892ra/720394.gif" alt=" photo kissingneck.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>.. *sigh*.. too much!!!<br>LOVED THIS STORY ALL OVER AGAIN!!!<br>READ IT!!! <br><br><i>Third read: August 4, 2014</i><br><br>Love!</span>

<div id="review_261470045" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/261470045" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/261470045?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-secondary-characters">wonderful-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=strong-willed-heroine">strong-willed-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=scrumptious-hero">scrumptious-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=passionate">passionate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=terrific-dialogue">terrific-dialogue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=awesome-alpha">awesome-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=laugh-out-loud-funny">laugh-out-loud-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=yummy-men">yummy-men</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer261470045" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6525567417445687508"><br/><b> 5 Stars!! Mystery Man is a mystery no more and he is definitely a superhero!!</b><br/><br/>I’m at a loss for words, other than Kristen Ashley blew me away AGAIN! Just when you think to yourself that she can’t out-do the possessive male jerk from the last book you read…WRONG…let me introduce you to Cabe “Hawk” Delgado. Even his name makes me swoon! Gwen is the object of his fascination and he was the object of mine. She is the consummate fashion plate, funny and as enamored with Cabe as he is with her. These </span>
  <span id="freeText6525567417445687508" style="display:none"><br /><b> 5 Stars!! Mystery Man is a mystery no more and he is definitely a superhero!!</b><br /><br />I’m at a loss for words, other than Kristen Ashley blew me away AGAIN! Just when you think to yourself that she can’t out-do the possessive male jerk from the last book you read…WRONG…let me introduce you to Cabe “Hawk” Delgado. Even his name makes me swoon! Gwen is the object of his fascination and he was the object of mine. She is the consummate fashion plate, funny and as enamored with Cabe as he is with her. These two slipped between the sheets every chance they got, and once again, major seat squirming on my part. Somehow when I read a KA book I find that I can’t sit still!! <br /><br />Gwen has a mind of her own, even if it that mind doesn’t think things through and it leads her straight to trouble. When she sets her sights on something there is no stopping her, and of course she does it in style, right down to her shoes. The girl is shoe-ho! <br /><br />I started out highlighting key parts to keep track of quotes and scenes that I liked; well that didn’t work out to well, because I damn near highlighted the whole book. I LOVED it ALL. At times I was laughing so hard that I thought I was going to choke. Warning, read this book in the privacy of your own home and not in public, or you might be at the receiving end of the Heimlich maneuver! <br /><br />Kristen Ashley writes such, that you read yourself right into the book. Her books are spot on when it comes to feelings, emotions, and circumstances. She always throws in that curve ball of unexpected, when revealing what came to pass in the history of her characters, this book being no exception. <br /><br />There was a whole troupe of secondary characters that I would love to see featured in future books. I don’t even feel right calling them secondary, it’s as if I do them a disservice, because they are front and center in the plot, shining stars in their own right. <br /><br />Have a box of Kleenex ready for the epilogue, another thing that KA does so well. It’s as if she herself needs this closure and she gifts it to her readers knowing we need it too. I had to read it twice, the first time it was blurred and after I wiped the wet away I read it again. I had a hard time putting this one away. <br /><br />I did have two issues wondering if I had missed something, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[what happened with Brett? Tack seemed to drop out of the story!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> or maybe I so absorbed with everything else that I’m just clueless. <br /><br />It’s on to Wild Man and hopefully some wild times!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6525567417445687508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14558919935898219913" style="display:none">★½ <br />The book starts with Gwendolyn "Gwen" Piper Kidd meeting a cute guy at a bar, taking him home and they had sex. They didn't talk. He started returning for a year and a half, always in the middle of night, without a key but somehow he got into her house.<br />Gwen didn't want to scare this sex god away, so she never asked him his name, how he gets into her house, nothing except "harder" or "faster". She nicknamed him Mystery Man "MM" when she talked to her friends.<br />None of her friends asked her WTF or slapped her, they just listened to the salacious stories she had to share about MM.<br /><br />When her sister gets Gwen caught up in her drama, MM decides to take care of his woman. unlike Gwen, MM (Cabe “Hawk” Delgado) did all his homework and knows all about her. So begins the journey to get to know each other outside the sack.<br /><br />She slept with him for 1½ years and didn't know his name nor what he looked like (she didn't recognize him when she saw him later) nor how he gets into her house/room---I JUST CAN'T PAST THAT. I tried, but I can't.<br />#notscaredofSTDs<br />#notscaredofmurderers</span>

Kristen Ashley is an obvious go-to girl as I tend to at least tolerate her characters/storylines and the pornbrarian has a bevy of options available for download. What I did not know was this was the introduction to the Chaos motorcycle club books that I h</span>
  <span id="freeText13314168763563466261" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a> <br><br>Last week I discovered Tik Tok and now most of my afternoons are spent looking like this . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589558065ra/29482301.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I figured it was high time to stop reading actual books and get something porny. Kristen Ashley is an obvious go-to girl as I tend to at least tolerate her characters/storylines and the pornbrarian has a bevy of options available for download. What I did not know was this was the introduction to the Chaos motorcycle club books that I have been splooshing over for years.<br><br><i>Mystery Man</i> is just that – a dude who picked our leading lady Gwen up in a bar a year and a half ago and who has been making occasional nighttime pleasure visits ever since. When Gwen finds herself caught up in a heap of trouble actually belonging to her sister, mystery man “Hawk” shows himself during daylight hours and stakes a claim on Gwen as his official woman. There’s only one problem – or make that two – Tack and Lawson, who both not only happen to have an involvement with the trouble brewing, but also an interest in our leading lady.<br><br>So there’s the basic plot, now let’s get to the important stuff that makes people read this shit in the first place . . . . .<br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589558065ra/29482302.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Okay, so first of all Cabe “Hawk” Delgado is some sort of former commando turned question-marky “good” guy who owns a security company, lives in a ginormous warehouse and drives hot cars. Basically, he’s . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589558065ra/29482303.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>(Ranger from the Stephanie Plums if you don’t read all the literary classics like I do.)</i> <br><br>And where there’s a Ranger, there has to be a Morelli, right? Enter Lawson the law man. (Think that’s lame? The other law guy’s name is Leo. Like Law Enforcement Officer? The creativity of KA is severely lacking.) When we meet him he’s described wearing a turtleneck so immediately all I could ever picture was . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589558065ra/29482304.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And in attempt to maybe do an anything you can do I can do . . . more of (????) there’s not two guys vying for Gwen’s attention, there’s . . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589558065ra/29482305.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Here comes Tack. He gets his own book with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1538647926?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a> later that really started me on this downward spiral of KA Kool-Aid drinking, but here he’s just one of the gang. He’s described with short hair and a long goatee of the salt-and-pepper variety, but I can’t help imagining this guy whenever he’s mentioned . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589558065ra/29482306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And don’t you judge me because back in the day Kevin Nash was fucking fly for a white guy and he’s also about 7 feet tall and probably has a huge ding-a-ling so just STFU.<br><br>So there you have it regarding the dudes. My complaints about the substance are the same per usual when it comes to these books: (1) They are WAAAAAY too long (and a true LOL moment came when the author not only plugged her own series (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2121935914?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a>), but also had Gwen (a book editor) say she would love a chance to work with the author. JFC – so do all of us readers. My kingdom for an editor to trim some of the fat!). (2) They are 100% formulaic with grunty caveman leading males who cannot speak in complete sentences and (again because they are never-fucking-ending) that gets tiring. (3) The sex is kind of terrible the more of them I read. I mean really these dudes are all supposed to be champs in the sack, but none of them know how to seal the deal without some external diddling???? (4) Break-up/make-up once is cool – three or four or seven times in one book is exhausting. But Imma still give it 4 Stars because I needed a timesuck and this delivered, I hopefully am not going to be on the predator watch list for continuing to watch questionably-aged young men airhump for me on the internets, I now know I will read the rest of this series, and Elvira was introduced in this one.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5938818710412613652">4.5 ALPHA-TASTIC STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417336i/825278._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Kristen Ashley is an 'Alpha male' writing goddess. I for one think this author deserves a Good Reads prize for handing out these Alpha goodie treats for the world to share!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417336i/825279._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I found myself in a bit of a book slump, and was kindly advised to get my reading bottom into gear and start the 'Dream man' series. So I decided to start a Kristen Ashley book binge, and OH yes what a book to start with, dream man I got. I loved this book ~<br/><br/> EVERY.SINGLE.ALPHA.LOVING. CHAPTER. <br/><br/>(so, thank</span>
  <span id="freeText5938818710412613652" style="display:none">4.5 ALPHA-TASTIC STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417336i/825278._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kristen Ashley is an 'Alpha male' writing goddess. I for one think this author deserves a Good Reads prize for handing out these Alpha goodie treats for the world to share!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417336i/825279._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I found myself in a bit of a book slump, and was kindly advised to get my reading bottom into gear and start the 'Dream man' series. So I decided to start a Kristen Ashley book binge, and OH yes what a book to start with, dream man I got. I loved this book ~<br><br> EVERY.SINGLE.ALPHA.LOVING. CHAPTER. <br><br>(so, thank you Good reads friends ~ you did GOOD)!<br><br>Where to start ~ FAB U LOUS characters, an influx of sexy men this heroine is lucky, lucky, lucky. (KA has an extremely fortunate imagination!). No insta love, HURRAY, Lisa happy dance. Instead a quirky, sexy and somewhat daring relationship between a YUMMY alpha bad boy (yes, I was getting squishy tummy right alongside the heroine). HAWK was THE best kind of book hero, gorgeous, overprotective and smart. coupled with a sassy upfront heroine with great one liners and more than enough attitude to make her a thoroughly enjoyable female lead.<br><br>I do have a teeny tiny wobble with this book, sometimes (just sometimes) I found the sentences and wording a bit bizarre and found myself re reading sentences to understand and it stopped the easy reading flow, but I loved this book all the same. <br><br>This book is fast paced and witty with a great storyline, romance and plenty of steam YIPPEE. It may not be for all readers, but check out the blurb, grab your kindle, sit back and prepare for some Biker boy action. This book is NOT short of drama, it was filled to the brim with mishaps and near death experiences. But reader do not fear, Kristen Ashley saved me from pulling out my hair with her chapter to chapter humour so it never felt too heavy or serious.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417336i/825280.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm in alpha heaven here. Loved it. Will 100% continue on this series with gusto.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417336i/825281.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4.5 Delicious 'HAWK' stars.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer305936206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6331568001882210927">This was my first KA <3 And a beginning of a beautiful friendship (addiction XD)<br/><br/>The story is an unusual one :) Gwen has a man that she only sees at night, they don't talk, she doesn't even know his name, but what she does know is that he's good in bed XD One day everything changes, her sister gets into a lot of trouble, and that forces Hawk to "come out". And when he does, Gwen decides to end things with him cause he esentially acts like a total jerk XD In the meantime, she meets Tack *drooling </span>
  <span id="freeText6331568001882210927" style="display:none">This was my first KA &lt;3 And a beginning of a beautiful friendship (addiction XD)<br /><br />The story is an unusual one :) Gwen has a man that she only sees at night, they don't talk, she doesn't even know his name, but what she does know is that he's good in bed XD One day everything changes, her sister gets into a lot of trouble, and that forces Hawk to "come out". And when he does, Gwen decides to end things with him cause he esentially acts like a total jerk XD In the meantime, she meets Tack *drooling all over my PC*, a biker guy who has the hots for her, and Mitch Lawson, a detective who also has the hots for her XD<br /><br />Aaanyway, Hawk and Gwen were great together, they had good times, getting to know each other <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ when they were at her parent's and the story how they met &lt;3  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, they had fights <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the worst was not when Hawk broke it off the first time, but after he told her everything and then broke it off ( I wanted to cry :( )  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, they made up &lt;3 <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ talking in the car about having kids &lt;3 I went all mush with that &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> there was some action and suspense <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the kidnapping, both of them  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but the epilogue did it for me &lt;3 It was just beautiful to read from Hawk's perspective &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 That's the most precious chapter here, loved it &lt;3<br /><br />I think there are too many hearts in this review loool but what can i say, it's just how I feel. And I'm glad I'm doing KA re-reads cause I know I can go no wrong with her, AND because in Mystery Man we get to see the dudes from Rock Chick, and Shirleen! When I first read it I had no idea who those people were.<br /><br />All in all 5+++ stars even for the second reading &lt;3</span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_17375956'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17375956-reaper-s-property"><img alt="Reaper&#39;s Property (Reapers MC, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1360943604l/17375956._SY160_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5RSVV/wYyz9v+dhfzhMm1XsKbtR3BZ1cWHYzN1GpIQn4ZIp2lLoeVV9tPWO3YbdP0TICkusR0fchOH0eQ9ehOg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UOZrPEU9wVSd5NDYvEnN4xjxh25Gr57h2B73n8nLGuVNlnQdLZ8UPq1wNeTFO1x5ssnrKNq70kqhULm227Wa1g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer5167977555391780398">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText5167977555391780398" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
